<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:остерегаться.html>остерега́ться</a> (15885)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">остерега́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">osteregátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:остерегаться.html>остерега́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">osteregátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">остере́чься</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to beware <i>(of)</i>, to be on one's guard <i>(against)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:остерегаться.html>остерега́йтесь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:падение.html>паде́ний</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>osteregájtesʹ</b> padénij</i> ― <span class="e-translation">mind (that) you don't fall</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:остерегаться.html>остерега́йтесь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вор.html>воро́в</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>osteregájtesʹ</b> voróv!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">beware of pickpockets!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:остерегаться.html>остерега́йтесь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дешевый.html>дешёвых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подделка.html>подде́лок</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>osteregájtesʹ</b> dešóvyx poddélok</i> ― <span class="e-translation">beware of cheap imitations</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">остерега́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">osteregátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***осторожно.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:осторожно.html>осторо́жно</a> (934)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">асцяро́жна</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ascjaróžna</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осторожно.html>осторо́жно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ostoróžno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>carefully, cautiously, with caution, with care</li>
<li>guardedly, warily</li>
<li>prudently</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осторожно.html>осторо́жно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ostoróžno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">short neuter singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осторожный.html>осторо́жный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ostoróžnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осторожно.html>осторо́жно</a>!</strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ostoróžno!</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>look out!, look sharp!, watch out!, be careful!
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:осторожно.html>осторо́жно</a></b>! <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>Ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чуть.html>чуть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поскользнуться.html>поскользну́лся</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Ostoróžno</b>! Ty čutʹ ne poskolʹznúlsja.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Look out</b>! You almost slipped.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>beware, danger!
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:осторожно.html>Осторо́жно</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:высокий.html>высо́кое</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:напряжение.html>напряже́ние</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Ostorožno</b>, vysókoje naprjažénije!</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Danger</b>! High voltage.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осмотрительный.html>осмотри́тельно</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">osmotrítelʹno</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осторожный.html>осторо́жный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ostoróžnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осторожность.html>осторо́жность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ostoróžnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осторожность.html>осторо́жности</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>care, caution, prudence
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обращаться.html>обраща́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:осторожность.html>осторо́жностью</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">obraščátʹsja s <b>ostoróžnostʹju</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">handle with care</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:осторожность.html>осторо́жности</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">iz <b>ostoróžnosti</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">out of prudence</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***осточертеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:осточертеть.html>осточерте́ть</a> (15470)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сто.html>сто</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sto</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:черта.html>черт</a>(<a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>е́й</a>)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čert(éj)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-étʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осточертеть.html>осточерте́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ostočertétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">осточертева́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make fed up, to make sick and tired <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ dative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:осточертеть.html>осточерте́ло</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">éto jemú <b>ostočertélo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is fed up with it</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:острейший.html>остре́йший</a> (24261)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:острый.html>о́стрый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">óstryj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́йший</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-éjšij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:острейший.html>остре́йший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ostréjšij</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:острый.html>о́стрый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">óstryj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:острый.html>о́стро</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">óstro</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:острота.html>остро́та</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ostróta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:острота.html>острота́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ostrotá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:острить.html>остри́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ostrítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***острить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:острить.html>остри́ть</a> (13782)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:острый.html>о́стрый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">óstryj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:острить.html>остри́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ostrítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to sharpen, to whet</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:острить.html>остри́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ostrítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сострить.html>состри́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be witty, to make witticisms, to crack jokes
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:острить.html>остри́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> че́й-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:счет.html>счёт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ostrítʹ</b> na čéj-libo sčót</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be witty at smb's expense; score off others</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:остров.html>о́стров</a> (1053)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ostrovъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*strow-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:остров.html>о́стров</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">óstrov</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:остров.html>о́строва</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:остров.html>острова́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:остров.html>острово́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>island</li>

<ol><li>частичн.: островершинный, <a href = vnd.unilang:остроконечный.html>остроконе́чный</a></li>
</ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***острый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:острый.html>о́стрый</a> (932)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ostrъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂ḱrós</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:острый.html>о́стрый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">óstryj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)остре́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)остре́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sharp, pointed</li>
<li>acute</li>
<li>keen</li>
<li>critical</li>
<li>hot, piquant <i>(of food, as pepper)</i></li></ol>
